  }%

\centering%
\setbox0=\hbox{%
\parbox{0.95\cardinnerwidth}{%
  \vspace{5pt}%
  \setstretch{0.8}%
  \fontsize{9}{10}\selectfont%
  \mbox{イチ}, \mbox{イツ} \\[2pt]%
  \mbox{ひと}, \mbox{ひと.つ} \\[2pt]%
  one, one radical (no.1)\\%
  \vspace*{\fill}\\[0pt]%
  \hspace*{\fill}\rule[0pt]{0.2\cardinnerwidth}{0.5pt}\hspace*{\fill}%
  一 : one%
  \hspace*{\fill}\rule[0pt]{0.2\cardinnerwidth}{0.5pt}\hspace*{\fill}\\[0pt]%
  \vspace*{\fill}%
  \fontsize{8}{9}\selectfont%
  \begin{multicols}{2}[]%
    %up to 6 compound meanings like '    \item [hiragana] [translation]'
    \begin{enumerate}[leftmargin=13pt,itemsep=1pt,parsep=2pt,topsep=2pt,partopsep=2pt,font=\normalfont\small]%
\item いち\\*
one
\item いっぽう\\*
one, the other, one way
\item ひとつ\\*
one
\item いちぶ\\*
one part, one portion, one section
\item いっぱん\\*
general, universal
\item いちにち\\*
one day\\
\end{enumerate}%
  \end{multicols}%
  \vspace*{\fill}%
}%
}%

\begin{flashcard}{

  \setbox0=\hbox{%
  \parbox{0.4\cardinnerwidth}{%
    \fontsize{10}{11}\selectfont
    %up to 6 compounds like '      \item ...'
    \begin{enumerate}[leftmargin=20pt,itemsep=1pt,parsep=2pt,topsep=2pt,partopsep=2pt,font=\normalfont\normalsize]
